=C2=A0 =C2=A0 =C2=A0 =C2=A0 =C2=A0 =C2=A0 =C2=A0 and analytic field is comp=
uted, as well as the relative error betw

=C2=A0een the mass

=C2=A0 =C2=A0 =C2=A0 =C2=A0 =C2=A0 =C2=A0 =C2=A0 of the source and destinat=
ion fields in the conservative case.
